	Dim mb_UseYT As Boolean

	Dim Ti1 As Object

	Dim fg_result_array_2(5) As Short
	Dim run_play_result_array_1(1, 14) As Short
	Dim rmtmp As Object
	Dim run_play_result_array_2(1, 38) As Short
	Dim rntmp As Object
	Dim break_away_result_array(38, 4) As Short
	Dim bytmp As Object
	Dim goal_line_result_array(38, 2) As Short
	Dim gltmp As Object

		frmtwominoff.Show()

	Private Sub cmdStopAutoSched_ClickEvent(ByVal eventSender As System.Object, ByVal eventArgs As System.EventArgs) Handles cmdStopAutoSched.ClickEvent
		gStopAutoPlay = True
		lvMain.Items.Add("Stopping AutoPlay...")
	End Sub
	
	Private Sub SSResizer1_BeforeResize(ByVal eventSender As System.Object, ByVal eventArgs As AxActiveResizer.DSSResizerEvents_BeforeResizeEvent) Handles SSResizer1.BeforeResize
		'    If Control.Name <> "Picture1" Then Exit Sub

		'    gResizeStarted = True
	End Sub
	
	Private Sub SSResizer1_ResizeComplete(ByVal eventSender As System.Object, ByVal eventArgs As System.EventArgs) Handles SSResizer1.ResizeComplete
		usrField.SetEndZoneName(team_name(0), 0)
		usrField.SetEndZoneName(team_name(1), 1)
		
		'    PrintEndZoneFont Picture1, team_name(0), 0, False
		'    PrintEndZoneFont Picture1, team_name(1), 1, False
		'    If Picture1.Width <= 7890 Then
		'        lvMain.Icons = imglistHelmets(0)
		'        lvMain.SmallIcons = imglistHelmets(1)
		'        lvMain.View = lvwReport
		'    Else
		'        lvMain.Icons = imglistHelmets(1)
		'        lvMain.SmallIcons = imglistHelmets(0)
		'        lvMain.View = lvwReport
		'    End If
		'    lvMain.ColumnHeaders.Item(1).Width = lvMain.Width
		'    DoEvents
		
		'UPGRADE_ISSUE: Line property linFieldStart.x1 is not supported at runtime. Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="74E732F3-CAD8-417B-8BC9-C205714BB4A7"'
		usrField.Left = VB6.TwipsToPixelsX(linFieldStart.x1)
		'UPGRADE_ISSUE: Line property linFieldStart.Y1 is not supported at runtime. Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="74E732F3-CAD8-417B-8BC9-C205714BB4A7"'
		usrField.Top = VB6.TwipsToPixelsY(linFieldStart.Y1)
		'UPGRADE_ISSUE: Line property linFieldEnd.Y2 is not supported at runtime. Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="74E732F3-CAD8-417B-8BC9-C205714BB4A7"'
		'UPGRADE_ISSUE: Line property linFieldEnd.x1 is not supported at runtime. Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="74E732F3-CAD8-417B-8BC9-C205714BB4A7"'
		'UPGRADE_ISSUE: Line property linFieldStart.Y1 is not supported at runtime. Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="74E732F3-CAD8-417B-8BC9-C205714BB4A7"'
		'UPGRADE_ISSUE: Line property linFieldStart.x1 is not supported at runtime. Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="74E732F3-CAD8-417B-8BC9-C205714BB4A7"'
		usrField.ResizeField(linFieldStart.x1, linFieldStart.Y1, linFieldEnd.x1, linFieldEnd.Y2)
		
		If VB6.PixelsToTwipsX(usrField.Width) <= 7890 Then
			lvMain.LargeImageList = imglistHelmets(0)
			lvMain.SmallImageList = imglistHelmets(1)
			lvMain.View = System.Windows.Forms.View.Details
		Else
			lvMain.LargeImageList = imglistHelmets(1)
			lvMain.SmallImageList = imglistHelmets(0)
			lvMain.View = System.Windows.Forms.View.Details
		End If
		'UPGRADE_WARNING: Lower bound of collection lvMain.ColumnHeaders has changed from 1 to 0. Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="A3B628A0-A810-4AE2-BFA2-9E7A29EB9AD0"'
		lvMain.Columns.Item(1).Width = VB6.TwipsToPixelsX(VB6.PixelsToTwipsX(lvMain.Width))
		
	End Sub

	'UPGRADE_ISSUE: UserControl event UserControl.InitProperties was not upgraded. Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="ABD9AF39-7E24-4AFF-AD8D-3675C1AA3054"'
	Private Sub UserControl_InitProperties()
		'UPGRADE_WARNING: Lower bound of collection lvMain.ColumnHeaders has changed from 1 to 0. Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="A3B628A0-A810-4AE2-BFA2-9E7A29EB9AD0"'
		lvMain.Columns.Item(1).Width = VB6.TwipsToPixelsX(VB6.PixelsToTwipsX(lvMain.Width))
		If Not DesignMode = True Then Exit Sub
		
		
	End Sub
	
	
	Sub PLAYGAME()
		
		
		For ipct = 0 To 1
			For z1 = 0 To 30
				dss(ipct) = dss(ipct) + defender_pct_of_sacks(ipct, z1)
			Next 
		Next 
		
		goal_posts_on_goal_line_flag = 0
		
		If pro_rules_using = 1 And using_pro_or_college_rules <> 0 Then
			goal_posts_on_goal_line_flag = -10
		End If
		
		If using_pro_or_college_rules = 4 Then
			goal_posts_on_goal_line_flag = 0
		End If
		
		
		
		
		If using_pro_or_college_rules <> 0 Then
			run_pass_pct(0) = run_pass_pct(0) + 2
			run_pass_pct(1) = run_pass_pct(1) + 2
		End If
		
		run_pass_pct(0) = run_pass_pct(0) + 4
		run_pass_pct(1) = run_pass_pct(1) + 4
		
		DISPWEATHER()
		If using_pro_or_college_rules <> 0 Then
			Call KickOff()
		Else
			Call ColKickOff()
		End If
	End Sub
	
	Private Sub StartGame()
		'p1 = d
		'd = 1 - p1
		'clear Globals
		'??????
		'gTeamYear(0) = ""
		'gTeamYear(1) = ""
		'gSeasonID(0) = ""
		'gSeasonID(1) = ""
		gAddImage = False
		gQuitGame = False
		gStatsComplete = False
		
		gDefLinePicked = False
		gDefCoverage = False
		gPreGame = False
		gGameTime = ""
		gGameTimeSelected = False
		DISPWEATHER()
		
340: 
		'p1 = d
		'd = 1 - p1
		Call MARKER1()
		x = 0
		u3 = 0
		If T <= 0 Then
			Call ADDTIME()
			GoTo 3360
		End If
		
		For i = 0 To 2
			If kor_pct_of_ret(d, i) = 100 Then
				kn = i
				GoTo krfound
			End If
			
		Next i
krfound: 
		i2 = Int(100 * Rnd(1)) + 1
		
		
		For i = 2 To 0 Step -1
			If i2 <= kor_pct_of_ret(d, i) Then
				i1 = i
			End If
			
		Next i
		RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1
		If kn = 1 And i1 = 1 Then kn2 = 0
		If kn = 1 And i1 = 0 Then kn2 = 1
		If kn = 2 And i1 = 1 Then kn2 = 0
		If kn = 2 And i1 = 0 Then kn2 = 1
		If kn = 0 Then
			pbp_display = kor_name(d, i1) & " (" & Str(Int(kor_ret_avg(d, i1) * 3)) & " AVG) is Deep to Receive the Kick"
			gHelmetImage = FindColor(d)
			Call pbp()
		End If
		
		If kn > 0 And RN <= 50 Then
			pbp_display = kor_name(d, i1) & " (" & Str(Int(kor_ret_avg(d, i1) * 3)) & " AVG) and " & kor_name(d, kn2) & " (" & Str(Int(kor_ret_avg(d, kn2) * 3)) & " AVG) ARE DEEP"
			gHelmetImage = FindColor(d)
			Call pbp()
		End If
		
		If kn > 0 And RN > 50 Then
			pbp_display = kor_name(d, kn2) & " (" & Str(Int(kor_ret_avg(d, kn2) * 3)) & " AVG) and " & kor_name(d, i1) & " (" & Str(Int(kor_ret_avg(d, i1) * 3)) & " AVG) ARE DEEP"
			gHelmetImage = FindColor(d)
			Call pbp()
		End If
		
		If mode_of_play = 1 And p1 = computer_control_flag Or mode_of_play = 2 Then
			i_dlr = "0"
			If T <= 180 And q = 4 And s(p1, 0) - s(d, 0) < 0 Then
				GoTo 3950
			Else
				GoTo 344
			End If
		End If
		
342: usrField.Show1stDownMarker(False)
		DISPWEATHER()
		ShowVbModal(frmtype_of_kickoff)
		If gQuitGame = True Then
			QuitPlay()
			Exit Sub
		End If
		
		
344: If i_dlr = "2" Then GoTo 3950
		If i_dlr = "1" Then GoTo 3970
		
		Call KICKSET()
		
		
		If n <= -9.99 Then
			Call CHANGEPOSS()
			GoTo 615
		End If
		x = 0
		If n < 0.01 Then GoTo 605
		n = n + (Int(Rnd(1) * 11) - 5) / 10
		y = n
		YT = 100 - y
		Call MARKER()
		Call yardline1()
		pbp_display = "KICK TAKEN BY " & kor_name(p1, i1) & " AT THE" & Str(Int(n + 0.5)) & " YD LINE "
		gHelmetImage = FindColor(p1)
		Call pbp()
		
450: RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 1000) + 1
		If kor_ret_avg(p1, i1) >= 10 And RN <= 80 Then
			g = 110
			GoTo 452
		End If
		
		If kor_ret_avg(p1, i1) >= 10 Then
			g = Int((Rnd(1) * 19) + 15) + (kor_ret_avg(p1, i1) - 10) * 3
			GoTo 452
		End If
		
		If kor_ret_avg(p1, i1) = 9 And RN <= 50 Then
			g = 110
			GoTo 452
		End If
		
		If kor_ret_avg(p1, i1) = 9 Then
			g = Int((Rnd(1) * 19) + 15)
			GoTo 452
		End If
		
		If kor_ret_avg(p1, i1) <= 8 And RN <= 5 Then
			g = 110
			GoTo 452
		End If
		
		If kor_ret_avg(p1, i1) <= 8 And RN <= 20 Then
			g = Int((Rnd(1) * 21) + 45) + (kor_ret_avg(p1, i1) - 7) * 3
			GoTo 452
		End If
		
		If kor_ret_avg(p1, i1) <= 8 And RN <= 70 Then
			g = Int((Rnd(1) * 21) + 25) + (kor_ret_avg(p1, i1) - 7) * 3
			GoTo 452
		End If
		
		If kor_ret_avg(p1, i1) <= 8 Then
			g = Int((Rnd(1) * 10) + 15) + (kor_ret_avg(p1, i1) - 7) * 3
			GoTo 452
		End If
		
452: Call YARDAGE()
		sy = 100 - y
		ey = sy - g
		Call MOVEBALL() 'move ball down the field
		x1 = 3
		kor_returns(p1, i1) = kor_returns(p1, i1) + 1
		If g + n > 89.99 Then
			kor_return_yds(p1, i1) = kor_return_yds(p1, i1) + 100 - n
			kor_return_td(p1, i1) = kor_return_td(p1, i1) + 1
			'UPGRADE_ISSUE: GoSub statement is not supported. Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="C5A1A479-AB8B-4D40-AAF4-DB19A2E5E77F"'
			GoSub 3637
			GoTo 3200
		End If
		
		If n + g <= -0.05 Then
			Call CHANGEPOSS()
			GoTo 615
		End If
		
		y = n + g
		If g > kor_return_lg(p1, i1) Then
			kor_return_lg_td_flag(p1, i1) = ""
			kor_return_lg(p1, i1) = g
			pbp_display = "Returned for " & Str(Int(g + 0.05)) & " Yards"
			gHelmetImage = FindColor(p1)
			Call pbp()
			pbp_display = "to the " & Str(Int(g + n + 0.05)) & " Yard Line"
			gAddImage = False
			Call pbp()
		End If
		
		kor_return_yds(p1, i1) = kor_return_yds(p1, i1) + g
		FPCT = 3
		Call FUMBLE()
		If f9 = 1 Then GoTo 640
		tp = Int(Rnd(1) * 3 + 4)
		T = T - tp
		'UPGRADE_WARNING: Couldn't resolve default property of object TIME_OF_POSS(). Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="6A50421D-15FE-4896-8A1B-2EC21E9037B2"'
		'UPGRADE_WARNING: Couldn't resolve default property of object TIME_OF_POSS(p1). Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="6A50421D-15FE-4896-8A1B-2EC21E9037B2"'
		TIME_OF_POSS(p1) = TIME_OF_POSS(p1) + tp
		i = Int(Rnd(1) * 1000) + 1
		If i >= 960 - team_penalty_adj(p1) Then Call CLIPPING()
463: Call ADDTIME()
		If T <= 0 Then
			Call ADDTIME()
			GoTo 3360
		End If
		GoTo 700
		
		
605: y = -(n - 2 * n)
		YT = 100 - y
		Call MARKER()
		Call yardline1()
		If mode_of_play = 2 Then
			If n < -2 Then
				i_dlr = "1"
			Else
				i_dlr = "0"
			End If
		Else
			If n < -2 Then
				i_dlr = "1"
			Else
				ShowVbModal(frmkick_ret_choice)
			End If
		End If
		
610: If Val(i_dlr) = 1 Then Call CHANGEPOSS()
		If Val(i_dlr) <> 1 Then GoTo 450
615: Call CHANGEPOSS()
		y = 20
		YT = 80
		Y1 = 10
		D1 = 1
		pbp_display = "TOUCHBACK"
		gAddImage = True
		gHelmetImage = gTouchBack
		Call pbp()
		Call MARKER()
		Call yardline1()
		GoTo 700
		
640: RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 6) + 1
		If RN = 1 Then pbp_display = "*** FUMBLE ON THE PLAY!! ***"
		If RN = 2 Then pbp_display = "*** LOOSE BALL!! ***"
		If RN = 3 Then pbp_display = "*** BALL IS ON THE GROUND!! ***"
		If RN = 4 Then pbp_display = "*** BALL IS KNOCKED LOOSE!! ***"
		If RN = 5 Then pbp_display = "*** BALL IS STRIPPED!! ***"
		If RN = 6 Then pbp_display = "*** FREE BALL !! ***"
		gAddImage = True
		If RN >= 1 And RN <= 6 Then gHelmetImage = gFumble
		Call pbp()
650: i6 = Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1
		team_fumbles(p1) = team_fumbles(p1) + 1
		If i6 <= 50 Then
			Call PBPINT()
			pbp_display = pbp_display & team_name(d) & " RECOVERS!!"
			gHelmetImage = FindColor(d)
			Call pbp()
			D1 = 1
			Y1 = 10
			team_fum_lost(p1) = team_fum_lost(p1) + 1
			y = 100 - y
			Call CHANGEPOSS()
			GoTo 659
		End If
		
652: If i6 <= 50 And y >= 90 Then Y1 = 100 - y
		If i6 > 50 Then
			pbp_display = team_name(p1) & " RECOVERS!!"
			gHelmetImage = FindColor(p1)
			Call pbp()
			i = 50
			o = 1
			GoTo 3303
		End If
		
		o = 5
		'UPGRADE_ISSUE: GoSub statement is not supported. Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="C5A1A479-AB8B-4D40-AAF4-DB19A2E5E77F"'
		GoSub 3900
		If OVERTIME_FLAG = 3 And q > 4 Then GoTo 3364
		GoTo 700
		
659: If using_pro_or_college_rules = 0 And COLLEGE_RULES_USING < 5 Then GoTo 652
		i = Int(Rnd(1) * 3) + 1
		If i <= 2 Then GoTo 652
		g1 = Int(Rnd(1) * 48) + 1
		x1 = 10
		If g1 >= 46 Then
			g1 = 100
			GoTo 667
		End If
		
		g1 = Int(Rnd(1) * 18)
667: g1 = g1 + (Int(Rnd(1) * 11) - 5) / 10
		pbp_display = "Returned for "
		If g1 + y >= 99.99 Then
			pbp_display = pbp_display & Str(Int((100 - y) * 10 + 0.5) / 10) & " YDS "
			gHelmetImage = FindColor(p1)
			Call pbp()
			GoTo 3200
		End If
		
		If g1 + y < 99.99 Then
			pbp_display = pbp_display & Str(Int((g1) * 10 + 0.5) / 10) & " YDS"
			gHelmetImage = FindColor(p1)
			Call pbp()
		End If
		
		If g1 + y <= 0.01 Then GoTo 3250
		y = y + g1
		GoTo 652
		
700: Call MARKER1()
		Call DISPWEATHER()
		o = 0
		f9 = 0
		g = 0
		w5 = 0
		If u3 = 9 Then
			u3 = 0
			GoTo 340
		End If
		
		If T <= 0 Then
			Call ADDTIME()
			GoTo 3360
		End If
		
702: Call SCOREBOARD()
		
		'??? go get plays
		Call DEFMENU()
		If gQuitGame = True Then
			QuitPlay()
			Exit Sub
		End If
		
		GoTo 3117
		
703: If mode_of_play = 1 And p1 = computer_control_flag And (p2 = 12 Or p2 = 15) And y >= 85 Or mode_of_play = 2 And (p2 = 12 Or p2 = 15) And y >= 85 Then p2 = 11
		If t1(p1) > 0 And y > 80 And Int(Rnd(1) * 25) + 1 = 16 Then
			pbp_display = "THERE'S SOME CONFUSION AT THE LINE OF SCRIMMAGE"

1207: i1 = Val(i_dlr)

		If i1 = 2 Then Wx_pct(0) = 1 - d
		If i9 = 1 Then
			Call CHANGEPOSS()
			W_pct = 1 - W_pct
		End If
		
		GoTo 1216
		
1211: If i9 = 3 Then Wx_pct(0) = p1
		If i9 = 4 Then Wx_pct(0) = d
		If i9 = 5 Then
			p1 = d
			d = 1 - p1
			W_pct = p1
			Call KickOff()
			GoTo 1216
		End If
		
		Call swap()
		Call SCOREBOARD()
		If mode_of_play = 1 And p1 = computer_control_flag Or mode_of_play = 2 Then
			i1 = 2
			GoTo 1215
		End If
		
		ShowVbModal(frmcointoss_6)
		
		
		
1212: i1 = Val(i_dlr)
		
1215: If i1 = 1 Then Call CHANGEPOSS()
1216: '
		
	End Sub
	Sub swap()
		p1 = d
		d = 1 - p1
		
	End Sub
	Sub SCOUT()
		For i = 0 To 1
			i2 = 0
			i3 = 0
			i4 = 0
			i5 = 0
			i6 = 0
			
			For i1 = 0 To 9
				If i1 = 0 And rb_pct_of_receptions(i, i1) > 0 Then
					k3(i, 3) = k3(i, 3) + rb_pct_of_receptions(i, i1) * rb_receiving_avg(i, i1)
					i2 = rb_pct_of_receptions(i, i1)
				End If
				
				If i1 > 0 And rb_pct_of_receptions(i, i1) > 0 Then
					k3(i, 3) = k3(i, 3) + rb_receiving_avg(i, i1) * (rb_pct_of_receptions(i, i1) - i2)
					i2 = rb_pct_of_receptions(i, i1)
				End If
			Next i1
			
			For i1 = 0 To 5
				If receiver_pct_of_receptions(i, i1) > 0 Then
					k3(i, 3) = k3(i, 3) + receiver_receiving_avg(i, i1) * (receiver_pct_of_receptions(i, i1) - i2)
					i2 = receiver_pct_of_receptions(i, i1)
				End If
			Next i1
			
			k3(i, 3) = Int((k3(i, 3) * 3) / 100)
			i2 = 0
			i3 = 0
			i6 = 0
			For i1 = 0 To 9
				If i1 = 0 And rb_pct_of_carries(i, i1) > 0 Then
					k3(i, 0) = k3(i, 0) + rb_pct_of_carries(i, i1) * rb_rush_avg(i, i1)
					i2 = rb_pct_of_carries(i, i1)
				End If
				
				If i1 > 0 And rb_pct_of_carries(i, i1) > 0 Then
					k3(i, 0) = k3(i, 0) + rb_pct_of_carries(i, i1) * (rb_rush_avg(i, i1) - i2)
					i2 = rb_pct_of_carries(i, i1)
				End If
				
			Next i1
			
			For i1 = 0 To 3
				If i1 = 0 And qb_pct_of_throws(i, i1) > 0 Then
					k3(i, 1) = k3(i, 1) + qb_pct_of_throws(i, i1) * qb_comp_pct(i, i1)
					i2 = qb_pct_of_throws(i, i1)
				End If
				
				If i1 > 0 And qb_pct_of_throws(i, i1) > 0 Then
					k3(i, 1) = k3(i, 1) + qb_comp_pct(i, i1) * (qb_pct_of_throws(i, i1) - i2)
					i2 = qb_pct_of_throws(i, i1)
				End If
				
			Next i1
			
			For i1 = 0 To 3
				If i1 = 0 And qb_pct_of_throws(i, i1) > 0 Then
					k3(i, 2) = k3(i, 2) + qb_pct_of_throws(i, i1) * qb_int_pct(i, i1)
					i2 = qb_pct_of_throws(i, i1)
				End If
				If i1 > 0 And qb_pct_of_throws(i, i1) > 0 Then
					k3(i, 2) = k3(i, 2) + qb_int_pct(i, i1) * (qb_pct_of_throws(i, i1) - i2)
					i2 = qb_pct_of_throws(i, i1)
				End If
				
			Next i1
			
			If i = 0 Then i1 = 1
			If i = 1 Then i1 = 0
			k3(i, 0) = ((k3(i, 0) * 3) / 100) + ((def_rush_adj(i1)) * 3) ' Rem HAD (B6()+1)*3
			k3(i, 0) = Int(k3(i, 0) + 0.5) / 10
			k3(i, 1) = Int((k3(i, 1) / 100) + def_comp_adj(i1) + 0.5)
			k3(i, 2) = Int((k3(i, 2) / 100) - def_int_adj(i1) + 0.5)
			k3(i, 4) = (punter_rating(i) * 2) + 28
			k3(i, 5) = (kicker_fg_made_pct(i, kicker_in_game(i)) * 5) + 25
			k3(i, 6) = kicker_xp_made_pct(i, kicker_in_game(i))
			xe = def_yds_catch_adj(i1) / 100
			If xe < 0.5 Then xd(i1) = Int(xe * 30)
			If xe > 0.5 Then xd(i1) = Int(((1 - xe) * 30) * -1)
			k3(i, 3) = k3(i, 3) + xd(i1)
			i4 = i
			If i4 = home_or_neutral_site_flag Then
				k3(i4, 0) = k3(i4, 0) + 0.3
				k3(i4, 1) = k3(i4, 1) + 3
			End If
			
			If i4 <> home_or_neutral_site_flag And home_or_neutral_site_flag <> 2 Then
				k3(i4, 0) = k3(i4, 0) - 0.3
				k3(i4, 1) = k3(i4, 1) - 3
			End If
			
		Next i
	End Sub
	
	Sub HALFSTART()
		txtResults.Text = ""
		'lvMain.ListItems.Clear
		p1 = W_pct
		d = 1
		If p1 = d Then d = 0
		t1(0) = 3
		t1(1) = t1(0)
		y = 35
		YT = 65
		D1 = 1
		Y1 = 10
		yf = -Y1
		If using_pro_or_college_rules <> 0 And goal_posts_on_goal_line_flag < 0 Then
			y = 40
			YT = 60
		End If
		
		If using_pro_or_college_rules = 1 And pro_rules_using = 3 Or using_pro_or_college_rules = 4 Then
			y = 30
			YT = 70
		End If
		
		If using_pro_or_college_rules = 0 And COLLEGE_RULES_USING = 0 Then
			y = 40
			YT = 60
		End If
		
	End Sub
	
	Private Sub KickOff()
		
		Call SCOREBOARD()
		If mode_of_play = 1 And p1 = computer_control_flag Or mode_of_play = 2 Then
			i9 = 2
			GoTo 1005
		End If
		
		ShowVbModal(FRMCOINTOSS)
		
1001: 
		i9 = Val(i_dlr)
		
1005: 
		If i9 < 3 Then GoTo 1006
		If i9 > 2 Then GoTo 1011
1006: Call SCOREBOARD()
		If mode_of_play = 1 And d = computer_control_flag Or mode_of_play = 2 Then
			i1 = 1
			GoTo 1010
		End If
		
		ShowVbModal(frmcointoss_2)
		
1007: 
		i1 = Val(i_dlr)
		
1010: 
		Wx_pct(0) = d
		If i1 = 2 Then Wx_pct(0) = 1 - d
		If i9 = 1 Then
			Call CHANGEPOSS()
			W_pct = 1 - W_pct
		End If
		
		
		GoTo 1017
1011: If i9 = 3 Then Wx_pct(0) = p1
		If i9 = 4 Then Wx_pct(0) = d
		Call swap()
		Call SCOREBOARD()
		If mode_of_play = 1 And p1 = computer_control_flag Or mode_of_play = 2 Then
			i1 = 2
			GoTo 1015
		End If
		
		ShowVbModal(frmcointoss_3)
		
1012: 
		i1 = Val(i_dlr)
1015: 
		If i1 = 1 Then Call CHANGEPOSS()
1017: '
		
	End Sub
	
	Sub PLACEPBP()
		pbp_display = VB.Left(pbp_display, 76)
		txtResults.Text = txtResults.Text & vbCrLf & lblTime.Text & "-> " & pbp_display
		txtResults.SelectionStart = Len(txtResults.Text)
		
		If gPlayingAutoSched = True Then Exit Sub
		
		If gAddImage = False Then
			lvMain.Items.Add(pbp_display)
		Else
			'UPGRADE_WARNING: Lower bound of collection lvMain.ListItems.ImageList has changed from 1 to 0. Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="A3B628A0-A810-4AE2-BFA2-9E7A29EB9AD0"'
			'UPGRADE_WARNING: Image property was not upgraded Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="D94970AE-02E7-43BF-93EF-DCFCD10D27B5"'
			lvMain.Items.Add(pbp_display, gHelmetImage)
		End If
		gAddImage = False
		'UPGRADE_WARNING: Lower bound of collection lvMain.ColumnHeaders has changed from 1 to 0. Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="A3B628A0-A810-4AE2-BFA2-9E7A29EB9AD0"'
		lvMain.Columns.Item(1).Width = VB6.TwipsToPixelsX(VB6.PixelsToTwipsX(lvMain.Width))
		'UPGRADE_WARNING: Lower bound of collection lvMain.ListItems has changed from 1 to 0. Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="A3B628A0-A810-4AE2-BFA2-9E7A29EB9AD0"'
		'UPGRADE_WARNING: MSComctlLib.IListItem method lvMain.ListItems.EnsureVisible has a new behavior. Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="6BA9B8D2-2A32-4B6E-8D36-44949974A5B4"'
		lvMain.Items.Item(lvMain.Items.Count).EnsureVisible()
		
	End Sub
	
	Sub pbp()

	End Sub

	Sub DISPWEATHER()
		
		If Wx_pct(1) = 0 Then
			lblgamewind.Text = "None "
		End If
		If Wx_pct(1) = -7 Then lblgamewind.Text = "Light "
		If Wx_pct(1) = -15 Then lblgamewind.Text = "Strong "
		If Wx_pct(1) <> 0 And Wx_pct(0) = p1 Then lblgamewind.Text = lblgamewind.Text & " +"
		If Wx_pct(1) <> 0 And Wx_pct(0) <> p1 Then lblgamewind.Text = lblgamewind.Text & " -"
		
		If Wx_pct(4) = 0 Then lblgameweather.Text = "Good"
		If Wx_pct(4) = -3 Then lblgameweather.Text = "Rain/Snow"
		If Wx_pct(4) = -6 Then lblgameweather.Text = "Downpour/Blizzard"
	End Sub
	Sub yardline1()
		yardline = YT - CShort(YT > 50) * 100 - YT - YT
	End Sub

		If r0 <= 20 Then
			d2 = 10
			d3 = 3
		End If
		
		If r0 <= 5 Then
			d2 = 9
			GoTo 8960
		End If
		
8865: If y >= 90 And d3 = 5 Or Y1 < 7 And d3 = 5 Then d3 = 3
		GoTo 8866
8895: If s(p1, 0) - s(d, 0) > 0 Then GoTo 8899
		r0 = Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1
		d2 = 3
		If r0 <= 50 Then d2 = Int(Rnd(1) * 3) + 4
		r0 = Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1
		If r0 <= 33 Then d3 = 1
		If r0 > 33 And r0 <= 67 Then d3 = 2
		If r0 > 67 Then d3 = 5
		GoTo 8866
8899: r0 = Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1
		RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1
		If RN <= 50 Then d2 = 1
		If RN > 50 And RN <= 70 Then d2 = 2
		If RN > 70 And RN <= 94 Then d2 = 3
		If RN = 95 Then
			d2 = 9
			d3 = 10
			GoTo 8866
		End If
		
		If RN = 96 Then
			d2 = 10
			d3 = 9
			GoTo 8866
		End If
		
		If RN > 96 And RN <= 98 Then
			d2 = 9
			GoTo 8866
		End If
		
		If RN > 98 Then
			d2 = 10
			d3 = 7
			GoTo 8866
		End If
		
		If r0 <= 90 Then d3 = 1
		If r0 > 90 Then d3 = 2
		GoTo 8866
8867: r0 = Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1
		d2 = 1
		d3 = 1
		If r0 <= 50 Then
			d2 = 2
			d3 = 3
		End If
		
		If r0 <= 5 Then d2 = 4
		GoTo 8866
8960: RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1
		If RN <= 45 Then
			d3 = 7
			GoTo 8865
		End If
		
		If RN <= 90 Then
			d3 = 8
			GoTo 8865
		End If
		
		If RN <= 95 Then
			d3 = 9
			GoTo 8865
		End If
		
		d3 = 10
		GoTo 8865
		
8866: '
	End Sub
	
	Sub FirstDownMarker(ByRef y As Single, ByRef Togo As Single)
		Dim FirstMarker As Single
		FirstMarker = y + Togo
		'    If p1 = 0 Then
		'        linFirstDownmarker.x1 = ((FirstMarker * (Line1(10).x1 - Line1(0).x1)) / 100) + Line1(0).x1
		'        linFirstDownmarker.x2 = ((FirstMarker * (Line1(10).x1 - Line1(0).x1)) / 100) + Line1(0).x1
		'    Else
		'        linFirstDownmarker.x1 = Line1(10).x1 - ((FirstMarker * (Line1(10).x1 - Line1(0).x1)) / 100)
		'        linFirstDownmarker.x2 = Line1(10).x1 - ((FirstMarker * (Line1(10).x1 - Line1(0).x1)) / 100)
		'    End If
		'    linFirstDownmarker.Visible = True
		With usrField
			If p1 = 0 Then
				.Set1stDownMarker(((FirstMarker * (.dGoal1pos - .dGoal2pos)) / 100) + .dGoal1pos)
			Else
				.Set1stDownMarker(.dGoal2pos - ((FirstMarker * (.dGoal2pos - .dGoal1pos)) / 100))
			End If
			.Show1stDownMarker(True)
		End With
	End Sub
	
	Sub MARKER()
		Dim YardMarker As Single
		'mark ball and 10 yd marker on field
		'MARKER1
		'Exit Sub
		If gPlayingAutoSched = True Then Exit Sub
		If mb_UseYT = True Then
			YardMarker = 100 - YT
		Else
			YardMarker = y
		End If
		'    If p1 = 0 Then
		'        imgMarker.Left = ((YardMarker * (Line1(10).x1 - Line1(0).x1)) / 100) + Line1(0).x1 - 420 ' 420=imgMarker.Width
		'    Else
		'        imgMarker.Left = Line1(10).x1 - ((YardMarker * (Line1(10).x1 - Line1(0).x1)) / 100)   ' 420=imgMarker.Width
		'        'imgMarker.Left = 7200 - ((y / 10) * 720) + imgMarker.Width
		'    End If
		With usrField
			If p1 = 0 Then
				.SetBallMarker(((YardMarker * (.dGoal2pos - .dGoal1pos)) / 100) + .dGoal1pos - 420) ' 420=ball.Width
			Else
				.SetBallMarker(.dGoal2pos - ((YardMarker * (.dGoal2pos - .dGoal1pos)) / 100)) ' 420=ball.width
			End If
		End With
		''already commented out
		'    If p1 = 0 Then
		'        imgMarker.Left = 7200 - ((yardline / 10) * 720) - imgMarker.Width
		'    Else
		'        imgMarker.Left = ((yardline / 10) * 720)
		'    End If
		If p1 = 1 Then
			imgHomePos.Visible = False
			imgVisitorPos.Visible = True
		Else
			imgHomePos.Visible = True
			imgVisitorPos.Visible = False
		End If
		System.Windows.Forms.Application.DoEvents()
	End Sub
	
	Sub MARKER1()
		If gPlayingAutoSched = True Then Exit Sub
		'mark ball
		'    If p1 = 0 Then
		'        imgMarker.Left = ((y * (Line1(10).x1 - Line1(0).x1)) / 100) + Line1(0).x1 - 420 ' 420=imgMarker.Width
		'    Else
		'        imgMarker.Left = Line1(10).x1 - ((y * (Line1(10).x1 - Line1(0).x1)) / 100)   ' 420=imgMarker.Width
		'        'imgMarker.Left = 7200 - ((y / 10) * 720) + imgMarker.Width
		'    End If
		If p1 = 1 Then
			imgHomePos.Visible = False
			imgVisitorPos.Visible = True
		Else
			imgHomePos.Visible = True
			imgVisitorPos.Visible = False
		End If
		System.Windows.Forms.Application.DoEvents()
	End Sub
	
	
	
	Sub MOVEBALL()
		If delay_in_seconds = 0 Then GoTo 2155
		i_dlr = "He's at "
		If ey > sy Then GoTo 2151
		
		mb_UseYT = True
		For YT = sy To ey Step -1
			Call MARKER()
			u_factorial = VB.Timer()
			If mode_of_play <> 2 Then Wait(100)
			'While Timer < u_factorial + delay_in_seconds / 20
			'Wend
			Call yardline1()
			yardline_pct = yardline
			If YT <= 0 Then
				YT = ey
			Else
				If Int(yardline_pct / 10) * 10 = yardline_pct Then
					pbp_display = i_dlr & " the " & Str(yardline_pct)
					gAddImage = False
					Call PLACEPBP()
					i_dlr = ""
				End If
			End If
		Next YT
		mb_UseYT = False
		
		GoTo 2154
		
2151: mb_UseYT = True
		For YT = sy To ey
			Call MARKER()
			If mode_of_play <> 2 Then Wait(100)
			'u_factorial = Timer
			'While Timer < u_factorial + delay_in_seconds / 20
			'Wend
			Call yardline1()
			yardline_pct = yardline
			
			If YT <= 0 Then
				YT = ey
			Else
				If Int(yardline_pct / 10) * 10 = yardline_pct Then
					pbp_display = i_dlr & " the " & Str(yardline_pct) & " yard line"
					gAddImage = False
					Call PLACEPBP()
					i_dlr = ""
				End If
			End If
			
		Next YT
		mb_UseYT = False
2154: If YT <= 0 Then
			YT = 0
			GoTo 2156
		Else
			YT = YT + 1
		End If
		
		Call yardline1()
		RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 21) + 1
		If RN = 1 Then i_dlr = " is Tackled"
		If RN = 2 Then i_dlr = " goes Out of Bounds"
		If RN = 3 Then i_dlr = " is Hit"
		If RN = 4 Then i_dlr = " goes Down"
		If RN = 4 Then i_dlr = " is Gang Tackled"
		If RN = 5 Then i_dlr = " is Stopped"
		If RN = 6 Then i_dlr = " is Tripped Up"
		If RN = 7 Then i_dlr = " is wrapped Up"
		If RN = 8 Then i_dlr = " is Ridden Down"
		If RN = 9 Then i_dlr = " is Leveled"
		If RN = 10 Then i_dlr = " is Pulled Down"
		If RN = 11 Then i_dlr = " is Hauled Down"
		If RN = 12 Then i_dlr = " is Forced Out"
		If RN = 13 Then i_dlr = " is Snowed Under"
		If RN = 14 Then i_dlr = " is Thrown Down"
		If RN = 15 Then i_dlr = " is Popped"
		If RN = 16 Then i_dlr = " is Smacked"
		If RN = 17 Then i_dlr = " is Slammed"
		If RN = 18 Then i_dlr = " is Stopped"
		If RN = 19 Then i_dlr = " is Popped"
		If RN = 19 Then i_dlr = " Steps Out"
		If RN = 20 Then i_dlr = " is Pushed Out"
		If RN = 21 Then i_dlr = " is Knocked Out of Bounds"
		If YT >= 100 Then GoTo 2165
		If YT <= 0 Then GoTo 2156
		Call MARKER()
		pbp_display = "and he" & i_dlr & " at the" & Str(Int(yardline_pct)) & " Yard Line"
		GoTo 2155
		
2165: pbp_display = "The ball carrier" & i_dlr & " for a " & Str(Int(-y)) & " yard loss"
2155: Call pbp()
2156: '
	End Sub
	
	Sub SCOREBOARD()
		
		Call MARKER1()
		yf = -Y1
		YT = 100 - y
		
		Call yardline1()
		
		ti = T
		ti = ti + ti * CShort(ti < 0)
		i = Int(ti / 60)
		
		j = ti - i * 60
		lblTime.Text = i & ":" & VB6.Format(j, "00")
		lblQtr.Text = CStr(q)
		lblDown.Text = CStr(D1)
		lblToGo.Text = VB6.Format(Y1, "##.0")
		lblQtr.Text = CStr(q)
		lblDown.Text = CStr(D1)
		lblVisitorScore(1).Text = CStr(s(1, 1))
		lblVisitorScore(2).Text = CStr(s(1, 2))
		lblVisitorScore(3).Text = CStr(s(1, 3))
		lblVisitorScore(4).Text = CStr(s(1, 4))
		lblVisitorScore(0).Text = CStr(s(1, 0))
		lblHomeScore(1).Text = CStr(s(0, 1))
		lblHomeScore(2).Text = CStr(s(0, 2))
		lblHomeScore(3).Text = CStr(s(0, 3))
		lblHomeScore(4).Text = CStr(s(0, 4))
		lblHomeScore(0).Text = CStr(s(0, 0))
		'    FirstDownMarker y, Y1
		
		'lblVisitorScore(4).Caption = Format(Y1, "##.0k")
		If y <= 50 Then
			lblballon_whose.Text = "Own"
		Else
			lblballon_whose.Text = "Opp"
		End If
		
		lblballonyl.Text = VB6.Format(yardline, "##.0")
		FirstDownMarker(y, Y1)
		
	End Sub
	
	Sub DEFMENU()
		If mode_of_play = 1 And d = computer_control_flag Or mode_of_play = 2 Then
			Call DEFENSE()
			Call DEFGOALLINE()
			GoTo 3055
		End If
		
3056: j = 10
		
		'ShowVbModal frmDefLineCall
		Select_Defense()
		If gQuitGame = True Then
			QuitPlay()
			Exit Sub
		End If
		
3057: 
		If UCase(i_dlr) = "Q" Then
			'?? fix this
			'UPGRADE_ISSUE: UserControl method usrPlayGame.Cls was not upgraded. Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="CC4C7EC0-C903-48FC-ACCC-81861D12DA4A"'
			Cls()
			End
		End If
		'?? need something to say not allowed - this just loops forever
		If UCase(i_dlr) = "G" And y >= 94.999 Then
			d2 = 11
			GoTo 3055
		End If
		
		If UCase(i_dlr) = "G" Then
			MsgBox("Goal line not allowed - must be 5 yard line or less")
			'GoTo 3057
			GoTo 3056
		End If
		d2 = Val(i_dlr)
		If d2 < 0 Or d2 > 9 Then GoTo 3057
		d2 = d2 + 1
		If d2 = 5 Or d2 = 6 Then
			d2 = d2 + 4
			GoTo 3061
		End If
		
		If d2 > 6 And d2 < 11 Then d2 = d2 - 2
3061: j = 10
		
		'ShowVbModal frmcoverage
		Select_Pass_Coverage()
		If gQuitGame = True Then
			QuitPlay()
			Exit Sub
		End If
		
		
3062: 
		
		If UCase(i_dlr) = "B" Then
			d3 = 10
			GoTo 3065
		End If
		
		d3 = Val(i_dlr)
		If d3 < 0 Or d3 > 9 Then GoTo 3062
3065: d3 = d3 + 1
		If (d2 = 5 Or d2 = 6) And (d3 = 7 Or d3 = 9 Or d3 = 11) Then GoTo 3056
		If (d2 = 7 Or d2 = 8) And (d3 = 8 Or d3 = 10 Or d3 = 11) Then GoTo 3056
3055: ':
	End Sub
	
	Sub DEFGOALLINE()
		If y > 94.999 Then
			d2 = 11
			d3 = 1
		End If
		
	End Sub
	
	Sub LGPBP()

		If RN = 19 Then pbp_display = "He Pops Out There"
		If RN = 20 Then pbp_display = "He Sees a Break"

	End Sub

	Sub FGATT()
		dt = Int(117 + goal_posts_on_goal_line_flag - y + 0.5)
		If dt <= 19 Then kicker_fga_019(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) = kicker_fga_019(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) + 1
		If dt > 19 And dt <= 29 Then kicker_fga_2029(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) = kicker_fga_2029(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) + 1
		If dt > 29 And dt <= 39 Then kicker_fga_3039(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) = kicker_fga_3039(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) + 1
		If dt > 39 And dt <= 49 Then kicker_fga_4049(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) = kicker_fga_4049(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) + 1
		If dt > 49 Then kicker_fga_5059(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) = kicker_fga_5059(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) + 1
	End Sub
	
	Sub FGMADE()
		If dt <= 19 Then kicker_fgm_019(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) = kicker_fgm_019(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) + 1
		If dt > 19 And dt <= 29 Then kicker_fgm_2029(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) = kicker_fgm_2029(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) + 1
		If dt > 29 And dt <= 39 Then kicker_fgm_3039(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) = kicker_fgm_3039(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) + 1
		If dt > 39 And dt <= 49 Then kicker_fgm_4049(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) = kicker_fgm_4049(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) + 1
		If dt > 49 Then kicker_fgm_5059(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) = kicker_fgm_5059(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) + 1
		'UPGRADE_WARNING: Couldn't resolve default property of object nz(kicker_long_fg(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)), ). Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="6A50421D-15FE-4896-8A1B-2EC21E9037B2"'
		If dt > nz(kicker_long_fg(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)), "") Then kicker_long_fg(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) = CStr(dt)
	End Sub
	Sub TAKESAFETY()
		tp = Int(Rnd(1) * 3) + 4
		T = T - tp
		'UPGRADE_WARNING: Couldn't resolve default property of object TIME_OF_POSS(). Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="6A50421D-15FE-4896-8A1B-2EC21E9037B2"'
		'UPGRADE_WARNING: Couldn't resolve default property of object TIME_OF_POSS(p1). Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="6A50421D-15FE-4896-8A1B-2EC21E9037B2"'
		TIME_OF_POSS(p1) = TIME_OF_POSS(p1) + tp
		g = (y * -1) - 1
		team_rush_att(p1) = team_rush_att(p1) + 1
		team_rush_yds(p1) = team_rush_yds(p1) + g
		pbp_display = punter_name(p1) & " is Headed Out of the End Zone"
		Call pbp()
		s(d, q) = s(d, q) + 2
		s(d, 0) = s(d, 0) + 2
	End Sub
	
	Sub DELAY()
		If mode_of_play <> 2 Then GoTo 8412
		'sleep for delay_in_seconds
		
		For dl = 1 To delay_in_seconds
		Next 
8412: '
	End Sub
	
	Sub FINDINT()
		':FIND INT
		m5 = 0
		RN = Int(Rnd(1) * ddi(1 - p1)) + 1
		For z1 = 0 To 30
			m5 = m5 + defender_pct_of_ints(1 - p1, z1)
			If RN <= m5 Then
				xdlr = defender_name(1 - p1, z1)
				GoTo 3660
			End If
			
		Next z1
3660: '
	End Sub
	
	Sub YARDAGE()
		g = g + (Int(Rnd(1) * 11) - 5) / 10
	End Sub
	
	Sub PUNTYARDS()
		i3 = Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1
		y = y + g
		Call CHANGEPOSS()
		YT = y
		y = 100 - y
		Call yardline1()
		RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 1000) + 1
		If pr_ret_avg(p1, pr) >= 6 And RN > 900 And i2 <> 1 Then
			g = 110
			GoTo 3819
		End If
		
		If pr_ret_avg(p1, pr) >= 6 Then
			g = Int((Rnd(1) * 26) + 0) + (pr_ret_avg(p1, pr) - 6) * 3
			GoTo 3819
		End If
		
		If pr_ret_avg(p1, pr) = 5 And RN > 940 And i2 <> 1 Then
			g = 110
			GoTo 3819
		End If
		
		If pr_ret_avg(p1, pr) = 5 And RN > 900 Then
			g = Int((Rnd(1) * 39) + 12)
			GoTo 3819
		End If
		
		If pr_ret_avg(p1, pr) = 5 Then
			g = Int((Rnd(1) * 25) + 0)
			GoTo 3819
		End If
		
		If pr_ret_avg(p1, pr) <= 4 And RN > 988 And i2 <> 1 Then
			g = 110
			GoTo 3819
		End If
		
		If pr_ret_avg(p1, pr) <= 4 And RN > 900 And i2 <> 1 Then
			g = Int((Rnd(1) * 39) + 12) + (pr_ret_avg(p1, pr) - 3) * 3
			GoTo 3819
		End If
		
		If pr_ret_avg(p1, pr) <= 4 And RN > 50 Then
			g = Int((Rnd(1) * 14) + 0) + (pr_ret_avg(p1, pr) - 3) * 3
			GoTo 3819
		End If
		
		If pr_ret_avg(p1, pr) <= 4 Then g = Int((Rnd(1) * 6) - 5)
		
3819: x1 = 4
		Call YARDAGE()
		Call MARKER()
		pbp_display = "The ball is taken by " & pr_name(p1, pr) & " at the " & Str(Int(yardline))
		Call pbp()
		sy = 100 - y
		ey = sy - g
		Call MOVEBALL()
	End Sub
	
	Sub FAKEYARDS()
		pbp_display = "IT'S A FAKE!!! The UpBack is Running the Ball"
		Call pbp()
		RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1
		If i2 = 0 And RN <= 36 Then g = Int(Rnd(1) * 27)
		If i2 = 0 And RN > 36 Then g = Int(Rnd(1) * 6) - 2
		If i2 = 1 And RN <= 36 Then g = Int(Rnd(1) * 21)
		If i2 = 1 And RN > 36 And RN <= 90 Then g = Int(Rnd(1) * 11) - 4
		If i2 = 1 And RN > 90 Then g = 100 - y
		If i2 = 2 And RN <= 8 Then g = Int(Rnd(1) * 21)
		If i2 = 2 And RN > 8 Then g = Int(Rnd(1) * 7) - 7
		Call YARDAGE()
		o = 1
		sy = 100 - y
		ey = sy - g
		Call MOVEBALL()
		pbp_display = "The Upback Gained"
		Call pbp()

		Call pbp()
	End Sub
	
	Sub FUMBLE()
		f8 = Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1
		If rfpct = 1 Then
			f8 = f8 - 10
			rfpct = 0
			GoTo 3627
		End If
		
		If FPCT = 2 Then f8 = f8 + 1
		If p2 = 1 Then f8 = f8 + 2
		If p2 = 5 Then f8 = f8 - 1
		If p2 = 2 Then f8 = f8 - 1
		If FPCT = 1 Then f8 = f8 - 6
		If FPCT = 5 Then f8 = f8 + 2
		If FPCT = 4 Then f8 = f8 - 2

	End Sub
	
	Sub FLEA()
		i1 = QB_IN_GAME(p1)
		cpct = qb_comp_pct(p1, QB_IN_GAME(p1)) + Int(def_comp_adj(d)) - 4
		ipct = qb_int_pct(p1, QB_IN_GAME(p1)) + def_int_adj(d) + 5
		spct = 5
		RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1
		If d3 = 11 Then spct = 70
		If d3 = 9 Or d3 = 10 Then spct = 50
		If d3 = 7 Or d3 = 8 Then spct = 30
		If RN <= 25 Then g = Int(Rnd(1) * 50) + 51
		If RN > 25 Then g = Int(Rnd(1) * 15) + 35
		cp = Int(Rnd(1) * 16) + 35
		If has_flea_flicker_been_run(p1) > 0 Then
			cpct = 3
			ipct = ipct + 10
			If spct = 5 Then
				spct = 30
			End If
		End If
		
		has_flea_flicker_been_run(p1) = 1
		pbp_display = rb_name(p1, 0) & " Takes the Handoff"
		Call pbp()
		pbp_display = "HE TOSSES IT BACK TO " & qb_name(p1, QB_IN_GAME(p1)) & " FOR A FLEA FLICKER!!!"
		Call pbp()
		i3 = Int(Rnd(1) * 3)
		pbp_display = receiver_name(p1, i3) & " is Open Downfield"
		Call pbp()
		RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1
	End Sub
	
	Sub REVGAIN()
		pbp_display = qb_name(p1, QB_IN_GAME(p1)) & " Takes the Snap"
		pbp_display = pbp_display & " and Hands off to " & rb_name(p1, i1) & " On The Reverse!!"
		gHelmetImage = FindColor(p1)
		Call pbp()
		RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1
		If RN <= 20 And has_reverse_been_run(p9) = 0 Then
			g = (Int(Rnd(1) * 8) + 5) * -1
			rfpct = 1
		End If
		
		If RN > 20 And RN <= 80 And has_reverse_been_run(p9) = 0 Then g = Int(Rnd(1) * 11)
		If RN > 80 And has_reverse_been_run(p9) = 0 Then g = Int(Rnd(1) * 81)
		If has_reverse_been_run(p9) > 0 And RN <= 5 Then g = Int(Rnd(1) * 81)
		If has_reverse_been_run(p9) > 0 And RN > 5 And RN <= 55 Then g = Int(Rnd(1) * 11)
		If has_reverse_been_run(p9) > 0 And RN > 55 Then
			g = (Int(Rnd(1) * 8) + 5) * -1
			rfpct = 1
		End If
		
		has_reverse_been_run(p9) = 1
	End Sub
	
	Sub FAKERUN()
		pbp_display = "IT'S A FAKE!!! The Holder is Running the Ball"

		RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1

		o = 1

		ey = sy - g
		Call MOVEBALL()
		pbp_display = "The Holder Gained"
		
		x = 10
		x1 = 11
		If Int((g + y) * 10 + 0.5) / 10 >= 99.94999 Then pbp_display = pbp_display & Str(Int(100 - y))
		If Int((g + y) * 10 + 0.5) / 10 < 99.94999 Then pbp_display = pbp_display & Str(Int((g) * 10 + 0.5) / 10)
		pbp_display = pbp_display & " Yards on the Fake Run"
		Call pbp()
	End Sub

	Sub ARMADJUST()
		s2 = qb_comp_pct(p1, i1) + Int(def_comp_adj(d))
		If p1 = home_or_neutral_site_flag Then s2 = s2 + 3
		If p1 <> home_or_neutral_site_flag And home_or_neutral_site_flag <> 2 Then s2 = s2 - 3
		If y <= 40.001 Then pq = 3
		If y > 40.001 And y <= 80.001 Then pq = -2
		If y > 80.001 And y <= 85.001 Then pq = -4
		If y > 85.001 And y <= 90.001 Then pq = -10
		If y > 90.001 And y <= 95.001 Then pq = -26
		If y > 95.001 Then pq = -13
		s3 = pass_play_adj_array(1, p2 - 8, d3)
		pw = 0
		If Wx_pct(0) <> p1 And (p2 = 11 Or p2 = 14 Or p2 = 16 Or p2 = 17 Or p2 = 18) Then pw = Wx_pct(2)
		If Wx_pct(0) <> p1 And (p2 = 12 Or p2 = 15) Then pw = Wx_pct(3) + Wx_pct(6)
	End Sub
	
	Sub SCORE()
		x2 = x2 + 1
		time_of_score(x2) = T
		qtr_of_score(x2) = q
		If x1 <> 7 Then k1(x2, 1) = p1
		If x1 = 7 Then k1(x2, 1) = d
		k1(x2, 0) = x1
		k1(x2, 5) = 100 - y
		If x1 = 3 Then k1(x2, 5) = 100 - n
		If x1 = 8 Then k1(x2, 5) = 117 + goal_posts_on_goal_line_flag - y
		k1(x2, 2) = i1
		If x1 = 5 Or x1 = 12 Then k1(x2, 2) = z1
		k1(x2, 3) = i3
		If k1(x2, 5) < 1 Then k1(x2, 5) = 1
	End Sub

		'p1 = computer_control_flag Or i1 = 3 And mode_of_play = 1 And
		'd = computer_control_flag Then GoTo 3910

		ShowVbModal(frmtwominoff)
		i1 = Val(i_dlr)
		If i1 < 1 Or i1 > 5 Or (i1 = 2 Or i1 = 4 Or i1 = 5) And mode_of_play = 1 And p1 = computer_control_flag Or i1 = 3 And mode_of_play = 1 And d = computer_control_flag Then GoTo 3910

	End Sub
	
	Sub FGDIST()
		i9 = 0
		If Wx_pct(0) = p1 And Wx_pct(1) = -7 Then i9 = -7
		If Wx_pct(0) = p1 And Wx_pct(1) = -15 Then i9 = -15
		If Wx_pct(0) <> p1 And Wx_pct(1) = -7 Then i9 = 7
		If Wx_pct(0) <> p1 And Wx_pct(1) = -15 Then i9 = 15
		For i = 4 To 0 Step -1
			If y >= fg_result_array_2(i) + goal_posts_on_goal_line_flag + i9 Then
				f2 = fg_result_array_1(i) - ((9 - kicker_fg_made_pct(p1, kicker_in_game(p1))) * 5)
			End If
			If y >= 68 + goal_posts_on_goal_line_flag And y >= fg_result_array_2(i) + goal_posts_on_goal_line_flag + i9 Then
				f2 = f2 + (y - fg_result_array_2(i)) + goal_posts_on_goal_line_flag - 4 + i9
			End If
		Next i
		If f2 <= 0 Then f2 = 5
		If f2 >= 100 Then f2 = 95
	End Sub

	Sub PASSPBP()
		':*** PASS PLAY BY PLAY ***
		RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1
		If d3 >= 7 And RN <= 33 Then
			pbp_display = "BLITZ IS COMING...!!"
			Call pbp()
			GoTo 4906
		End If
		
		If d3 >= 7 And RN <= 66 Then
			pbp_display = "HERE COMES THE BLITZ...!!"
			Call pbp()
			GoTo 4906
		End If
		
		If d3 >= 7 Then
			pbp_display = "BLITZ IS ON...!!"
			Call pbp()
		End If
		
		If dss(1 - p1) = 0 Then
			xdlr = team_name(1 - p1)
			GoTo 4906
		End If
		
		m5 = 0
		RN = Int(Rnd(1) * dss(1 - p1)) + 1
		For z1 = 0 To 30
			m5 = m5 + defender_pct_of_sacks(1 - p1, z1)
			If RN <= m5 Then
				xdlr = defender_name(1 - p1, z1)
				GoTo 4906
			End If
			
		Next 
		
4906: RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 15) + 1
		If (d3 >= 7 Or d2 >= 9) And RN = 1 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " HAS TO HURRY"
		If (d3 >= 7 Or d2 >= 9) And RN = 2 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " IS UNDER A HEAVY PASS RUSH"
		If (d3 >= 7 Or d2 >= 9) And RN = 3 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " IS BEING RUSHED"
		If (d3 >= 7 Or d2 >= 9) And RN = 4 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " IS BEING PRESSURED"
		If (d3 >= 7 Or d2 >= 9) And RN = 5 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " FEELS THE HEAT"
		If (d3 >= 7 Or d2 >= 9) And RN = 6 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " IS BEING CHASED"
		If (d3 >= 7 Or d2 >= 9) And RN = 7 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " IS BEING HURRIED"
		If (d3 >= 7 Or d2 >= 9) And RN = 8 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " IS FORCED OUT OF THE POCKET"
		If (d3 >= 7 Or d2 >= 9) And RN = 9 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " IS SCRAMBLING"
		If (d3 >= 7 Or d2 >= 9) And RN = 10 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " IS UNDER THE GUN"
		If (d3 >= 7 Or d2 >= 9) And RN = 11 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & "'S POCKET IS COLLAPSING"
		If (d3 >= 7 Or d2 >= 9) And RN = 12 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & "'S PROTECTION IS BREAKING DOWN"
		If (d3 >= 7 Or d2 >= 9) And RN = 13 Then pbp_display = "HERE COMES " & xdlr
		If (d3 >= 7 Or d2 >= 9) And RN = 14 Then pbp_display = xdlr & " BREAKS THROUGH"
		If (d3 >= 7 Or d2 >= 9) And RN = 15 Then pbp_display = xdlr & " IS COMING THROUGH"
		
		If d3 >= 7 Or d2 >= 9 Then GoTo 4905
		
		If (p2 = 9 Or p2 = 10) And RN <= 50 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " Takes the Snap and Drops back...Looking Short..."
		If (p2 = 9 Or p2 = 10) And RN > 50 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " DROPS QUICKLY AND SETS..."
		If (p2 = 14 Or p2 = 15) And RN <= 50 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " MAKES A GOOD PLAY FAKE..."
		If (p2 = 14 Or p2 = 15) And RN > 50 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " FAKES THE GIVE AND WANTS TO THROW IT..."
		If (p2 = 11 Or p2 = 16) And RN <= 30 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " DROPS BACK AND LOOKS..."
		If (p2 = 11 Or p2 = 16) And RN > 30 And RN <= 40 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " DROPS BACK...HE'S UNDER PRESSURE..."
		If (p2 = 11 Or p2 = 16) And RN > 40 And RN <= 60 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " TO THROW...HAS TIME..."
		If (p2 = 11 Or p2 = 16) And RN > 60 And RN <= 70 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " BACK TO PASS...HAS PROTECTION..."
		If (p2 = 11 Or p2 = 16) And RN > 70 And RN <= 80 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " DROPS BACK...IS BEING CHASED!!"
		If (p2 = 11 Or p2 = 16) And RN > 80 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " HAS PLENTY OF TIME TO THROW..."
		If p2 = 13 And RN <= 50 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " DROPPING...BEING CHASED..."
		If p2 = 13 And RN > 50 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " DROPS BACK...HE'S UNDER PRESSURE..."
		If p2 = 17 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " ROLLS OUT..."
		If p2 = 18 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " HAS IT ON THE BOOTLEG"
		If p2 = 12 And RN <= 50 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " DROPS BACK...HE WANTS TO GO DEEP"
		If p2 = 12 And RN > 50 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1) & " TAKES A DEEP DROP...HE'S LOOKING LONG"
		gHelmetImage = FindColor(p1)
4905: Call pbp()
	End Sub
	
	Sub SACK()
		pbp_display = "BUT HE WON'T BE ABLE TO GET THIS PASS AWAY!"
		Call pbp()
		pbp_display = qb_name(p1, i1)
		If hbpct1 = 1 Then pbp_display = rb_name(p1, i1)
		If e = 1 Then
			pbp_display = pbp_display & " IS DROPPED"
			GoTo 4907
		End If
		
		RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 12) + 1
		If RN = 1 Then pbp_display = pbp_display & " IS SACKED"
		If RN = 2 And RN <= 20 Then pbp_display = pbp_display & " IS NAILED"
		If RN = 3 And RN <= 30 Then pbp_display = pbp_display & " IS BURIED"
		If RN = 4 And RN <= 40 Then pbp_display = pbp_display & " IS DRILLED"
		If RN = 5 And RN <= 50 Then pbp_display = pbp_display & " IS HIT"
		If RN = 6 And RN <= 60 Then pbp_display = pbp_display & " IS THROWN"
		If RN = 7 And RN <= 70 Then pbp_display = pbp_display & " IS HAMMERED"
		If RN = 8 And RN <= 80 Then pbp_display = pbp_display & " IS TACKLED"
		If RN = 9 And RN <= 90 Then pbp_display = pbp_display & " IS SWARMED UNDER"
		If RN = 10 Then pbp_display = pbp_display & " IS LEVELED"
		If RN = 11 Then pbp_display = pbp_display & " IS SNOWED UNDER"
		If RN = 12 Then pbp_display = pbp_display & " IS WRAPPED UP"
		
		
4907: pbp_display = pbp_display & " for a " & Str(Int(g + 0.5)) & " Yard Loss"
	End Sub
	Sub STUFFED()

	End Sub
	
	Sub MISSFG()
		dr = Int(Rnd(1) * 2)
		RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1
		If RN <= 35 Then pbp_display = "NO GOOD"
		If RN > 35 And RN <= 60 Then pbp_display = "IT SAILS WIDE...NO GOOD"
		If RN > 60 And RN <= 80 Then pbp_display = "HE MISSED IT!"
		If RN > 80 And RN <= 85 Then pbp_display = "IT HITS THE UPRIGHTS....NO GOOD!"
		If RN > 85 And RN <= 90 Then pbp_display = "HE HOOKS IT...NO GOOD!"
		If RN > 90 And RN <= 95 And 117 + goal_posts_on_goal_line_flag - y > 45 Then pbp_display = "IT FALLS SHORT....NO GOOD!"
		If RN > 90 And RN <= 95 And 117 + goal_posts_on_goal_line_flag - y <= 45 Then pbp_display = "IT'S NO GOOD ... OFF TO THE " & dir_dlr(dr)
		If RN > 95 Then pbp_display = "IT'S NO GOOD!"
		gHelmetImage = gFieldGoalNo
		gAddImage = True
		Call pbp()
	End Sub

	Sub MISSPAT()

		If RN > 95 Then pbp_display = "IT HITS THE UPRIGHTS!!...NO GOOD!"

		gAddImage = True

	End Sub

	Sub KICKSET()
		pbp_display = kicker_name(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) & " is Placing the Ball on the Tee"
		gHelmetImage = FindColor(p1)
		Call pbp()
		RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1
		
		pbp_display = team_name(p1) & " IS LINING UP FOR THE KICKOFF"
		Call pbp()
		pbp_display = "AND THE KICK IS ON ITS WAY"
		Call pbp()
		Call swap()
		RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1
		':*** added +goal_posts_on_goal_line_flag to the next 2 lines ***
		If RN <= 88 Then n = 100 - (y + Int(Rnd(1) * 13) + 55 + goal_posts_on_goal_line_flag)
		If RN > 88 Then n = 100 - (y + Int(Rnd(1) * 8) + 68 + goal_posts_on_goal_line_flag)
		If using_pro_or_college_rules = 0 And COLLEGE_RULES_USING = 0 Then n = n + 10
		If Wx_pct(0) = p1 Then n = n - Int(Rnd(1) * 7) + 3 - Wx_pct(1)
		If Wx_pct(0) <> p1 Then n = n + Int(Rnd(1) * 7) - 3 + Wx_pct(1)
	End Sub
	
	Sub QBTHROW()
		RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1
		If RN = 1 Then pbp_display = "HE PASSES IT"
		If RN = 2 Then pbp_display = "HE FIRES IT"
		If RN = 3 Then pbp_display = "HE FIRES THE BALL"
		If RN = 4 Then pbp_display = "HE FIRES ONE"
		If RN = 5 Then pbp_display = "HE FIRES A PASS"
		If RN = 6 Then pbp_display = "HE RIFLES IT"
		If RN = 7 Then pbp_display = "HE RIFLES THE BALL"
		If RN = 8 Then pbp_display = "HE RIFLES ONE"
		If RN = 9 Then pbp_display = "HE RIFLES A PASS"
		If RN = 10 Then pbp_display = "HE THROWS"
		If RN = 11 Then pbp_display = "HE TOSSES"
		If RN = 12 Then pbp_display = "HE DRILLS A PASS"
		If RN = 13 Then pbp_display = "HE FLOATS A PASS"
		If RN = 14 Then pbp_display = "HE THREADS IT"
		If RN = 15 Then pbp_display = "HE DRILLS THE BALL"
		If RN = 16 Then pbp_display = "HE UNLOADS THE BALL"
		If RN = 17 Then pbp_display = "HE UNLOADS IT"
		If RN = 18 Then pbp_display = "HE RIPS THE BALL"
		If RN = 19 Then pbp_display = "HE RIPS IT"
		If RN = 20 Then pbp_display = "THROWN ON A LINE"
		If RN = 21 Then pbp_display = "HE DRILLS IT"
		If RN = 22 Then pbp_display = "HE FLINGS IT"
		If RN = 23 Then pbp_display = "HE FIRES A BULLET"
		If RN <= 23 Then Call pbp()
	End Sub

	Sub PCPBP()
		Call QBTHROW()
4150: If ffpct <> 0 Then GoTo 4165
		If p2 = 13 And ry < 3 Then
			cp = Int(Rnd(1) * 4) - 7
			GoTo 4165
		End If
		
		If p2 = 13 Then
			cp = (Int(Rnd(1) * 4) + 1) * -1
			GoTo 4165
		End If
		
		If (p2 = 9 Or p2 = 10) And ry < 3 Then
			cp = Int(Rnd(1) * 7) - 2
			GoTo 4165
		End If
		
		If (p2 = 9 Or p2 = 10) Then
			cp = Int(Rnd(1) * 6) + 2
			GoTo 4165
		End If
		
		If (p2 = 11 Or p2 = 14 Or p2 = 16 Or p2 = 17 Or p2 = 18) And ry < 4 Then
			cp = Int(Rnd(1) * 5) + 3
			GoTo 4165
		End If
		
		
		If (p2 = 11 Or p2 = 14 Or p2 = 16 Or p2 = 17 Or p2 = 18) And ry < 6 Then
			cp = Int(Rnd(1) * 9) + 6
			GoTo 4165
		End If
		
		
		If (p2 = 11 Or p2 = 14 Or p2 = 16 Or p2 = 17 Or p2 = 18) Then
			cp = Int(Rnd(1) * 9) + 8
			GoTo 4165
		End If
		
		
		If (p2 = 12 Or p2 = 15) And ry < 3 Then
			cp = Int(Rnd(1) * 5) + 3
			GoTo 4165
		End If
		
		If (p2 = 12 Or p2 = 15) And ry < 5 Then
			cp = Int(Rnd(1) * 10) + 10
			GoTo 4165
		End If
		
		cp = Int(Rnd(1) * 36) + 20
4165: pc = cp
		If cp > g Then
			cp = g
			it = 1
		End If
		
		YT = 100 - y - cp
		Call yardline1()
		Call MARKER()
		If YT <= 0 Then
			pbp_display = rv_dlr & " MAKES THE CATCH IN THE END ZONE!!!"
			Call pbp()
			GoTo 4175
		End If
		
		RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1
		
		If (p2 = 9 Or p2 = 10) And RN <= 33 Then pbp_display = rv_dlr & " has it over the Middle"
		If (p2 = 9 Or p2 = 10) And RN > 33 And RN <= 67 Then pbp_display = rv_dlr & " Catches it in the Flat"
		If (p2 = 9 Or p2 = 10) And RN > 67 Then pbp_display = "He Dumps it to " & rv_dlr
		
		If (p2 = 11 Or p2 = 12 Or p2 = 14 Or p2 = 15) And RN <= 33 Then
			pbp_display = rv_dlr & " Takes it over the Middle"
		End If
		If (p2 = 11 Or p2 = 12 Or p2 = 14 Or p2 = 15) And RN > 33 And RN <= 67 Then
			pbp_display = "HE HAS " & rv_dlr
		End If
		If (p2 = 11 Or p2 = 12 Or p2 = 14 Or p2 = 15) And RN > 67 Then pbp_display = "He Completes it to " & rv_dlr
		
		If p2 = 16 And RN <= 50 Then pbp_display = "He has " & rv_dlr & " near the Sideline"
		If p2 = 16 And RN > 50 Then pbp_display = "He finds " & rv_dlr
		
		If p2 = 13 And RN <= 33 Then pbp_display = "He Screens it to " & rv_dlr
		If p2 = 13 And RN > 33 And RN <= 67 Then pbp_display = "He Dumps the Screen to " & rv_dlr
		If p2 = 13 And RN > 67 Then pbp_display = "He has " & rv_dlr & " on the Screen Pass"
		
		If (p2 = 17 Or p2 = 18) And RN <= 50 Then pbp_display = "He Hits " & rv_dlr
		If (p2 = 17 Or p2 = 18) And RN > 50 And RN <= 90 Then pbp_display = "He Fires it to " & rv_dlr
		
		If ffpct <> 0 Or (p2 = 17 Or p2 = 18) And RN > 90 Then pbp_display = rv_dlr & " makes a Great Catch"
		
		pbp_display = pbp_display & " at the" & Str(Int(yardline)) & " Yard line"
		If it = 1 Then
			it = 0
			Call pbp()
			Call pbp()
			GoTo 4175
		End If
		
		
		Call pbp()
		sy = 100 - y - cp
		ey = 100 - y - g
		Call MOVEBALL()
4175: '
	End Sub
	Sub QBLINE()
		Qb = CStr(0)
		dndlr(1) = "First"
		dndlr(2) = "Second"
		dndlr(3) = "Third"
		dndlr(4) = "Fourtn"
		If random_qb_select_flag(p1) = 1 Then
			QB_IN_GAME(p1) = 0
		Else
			Qb = CStr(QB_IN_GAME(p1))
		End If
		
		If D1 <= 2 Or D1 = 3 And Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1 <= 80 Then GoTo 4100
		RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 8) + 1
		If RN = 1 Then pbp_display = team_name(p1) & " Comes up to the Line"
		If RN = 2 Then pbp_display = team_name(p1) & " Breaks the Huddle and Lines Up"
		If RN = 3 Then pbp_display = "They " & aa_dlr(p1) & " Come up to the Line"
		If RN = 4 Then pbp_display = "They " & aa_dlr(p1) & " Break the Huddle and Line Up"
		If RN = 5 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, CInt(Qb)) & " Barks out the signals"
		If RN = 6 Then pbp_display = qb_name(p1, CInt(Qb)) & " Looks over the Defense"
		If RN = 7 Then pbp_display = "Here is the " & dndlr(D1) & " Down and" & Str(Int(Y1)) & " Yard Play for " & team_name(p1)
		If RN = 8 Then pbp_display = "Here is the " & dndlr(D1) & " Down and" & Str(Int(Y1)) & " Yard Play for the " & aa_dlr(p1)
		Call pbp()
4100: '
	End Sub
	
	Sub SQUIB()
		pbp_display = kicker_name(p1, kicker_in_game(p1)) & " is placing the ball on the Tee"
		gHelmetImage = FindColor(p1)
		Call pbp()
		pbp_display = team_name(p1) & " is lining up for the Kickoff"
		Call pbp()
		pbp_display = "It's a Squibber down the Field"
		Call pbp()
		Call swap()
		n = 100 - (y + Int(Rnd(1) * 16) + 29)
		x = 0
		n = n + (Int(Rnd(1) * 11) - 5) / 10
		y = n
		YT = 100 - y
		Call MARKER()
		Call yardline1()
		pbp_display = "Kick taken by an Upman at the " & Str(Int(n + 0.5)) & " Yard Line "
		Call pbp()
		g = Int(Rnd(1) * 7) + 9
		sy = 100 - y
		ey = sy - g
		Call MOVEBALL()
		pbp_display = "returned " & Str(Int(g)) & " yards"
		Call pbp()
		y = n + g
		FPCT = 3
	End Sub
	
	Sub PUNTPBP()
		RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 12) + 1
		If RN = 1 Then pbp_display = "HE HITS IT"
		If RN = 2 Then pbp_display = "HE NAILS IT"
		If RN = 3 Then pbp_display = "HE KICKS IT"
		If RN = 4 Then pbp_display = "HE LAUNCHES IT"
		If RN = 5 Then pbp_display = "HE BOOTS IT"
		If RN = 6 Then pbp_display = "HE BOOMS IT"
		If RN = 7 Then pbp_display = "HE HITS ONE"
		If RN = 8 Then pbp_display = "HE NAILS ONE"
		If RN = 9 Then pbp_display = "HE KICKS ONE"
		If RN = 10 Then pbp_display = "HE LAUNCHES ONE"
		If RN = 11 Then pbp_display = "HE BOOTS ONE"
		If RN = 12 Then pbp_display = "HE BOOMS ONE"
		Call pbp()
		RN = Int(Rnd(1) * 6) + 1
		If RN = 1 Then pbp_display = "IT'S A HIGH, SPIRALING KICK"
		If RN = 2 Then pbp_display = "IT'S A HIGH FLOATER"
		If RN = 3 Then pbp_display = "IT'S A HIGH END OVER END KICK"
		If RN = 4 Then pbp_display = "IT'S A LOW, LINE DRIVE"
		If RN = 5 Then pbp_display = "HE GETS IT TO TURN OVER"
		If RN = 6 Then pbp_display = "HE DOESN'T GET IT TO TURN OVER"
	End Sub
	
	
	
	Sub MEASUREMENT()
		':MEASUREMENT
		pbp_display = "HE'S CLOSE TO A FIRST DOWN"
		Call pbp()
		pbp_display = "THE OFFICIAL SIGNALS FOR A MEASUREMENT"
		Call pbp()
		If g - Y1 < -0.2 Then
			pbp_display = "HE'S ABOUT A FOOT SHORT"
			GoTo 3427
		End If
		
		If g - Y1 < -0.1 Then
			pbp_display = "HE'S ABOUT 6 INCHES SHORT"
			GoTo 3427
		End If
		
		If g - Y1 <= -0.01 Then
			pbp_display = "HE'S SHORT BY INCHES"
			GoTo 3427
		End If
		
		pbp_display = "THE OFFICIAL SIGNALS FIRST DOWN!"
3427: Call pbp()
	End Sub
	
	Sub WHICHRECEIVER()
		If i3 > 9 Then
			pbp_display = pbp_display & receiver_name(p1, i3 - 10)
		Else
			pbp_display = pbp_display & rb_name(p1, i3)
		End If
		
	End Sub
	
	Sub CLIPPING()
		pbp_display = "*** PENALTY - 10 YD ILLEGAL BLOCK ON THE RETURN ***"
		Call pbp()
		If y < 20 Then
			y = y / 2
			team_penalty_yds(p1) = team_penalty_yds(p1) + y / 2
		End If
		
		team_penalties(p1) = team_penalties(p1) + 1
		If y >= 20 Then
			y = y - 10
			team_penalty_yds(p1) = team_penalty_yds(p1) + 10
		End If
		
	End Sub
	
	
	Sub CHANGEQB()
		
		If mode_of_play = 2 Or mode_of_play = 1 And computer_control_flag = p1 Then
			i = Int(Rnd(1) * 100) + 1
			For i2 = 3 To 0 Step -1
				If i <= qb_pct_of_throws(p1, i2) Then i1 = i2
			Next i2
			QB_IN_GAME(p1) = i1
			
		Else
			ShowVbModal(frmSelectQB)
		End If
		
		
		
8320: For i = 0 To 3
			v4pct(i3, i) = -1
		Next i
		If random_qb_select_flag(i3) = 1 Then GoTo 8325
		For i4 = 0 To 9
			For i5 = 0 To 3
				If rb_name(i3, i4) = qb_name(i3, i5) And i5 <> QB_IN_GAME(i3) Then v4pct(i3, i5) = i4
			Next i5
		Next i4
8325: '
	End Sub
	
	
	Sub CHANGEPOSS()
		Call swap()
	End Sub

	Private Sub QuitPlay()
		lvMain.Items.Add("Quitting Game...")
		'UPGRADE_WARNING: Lower bound of collection lvMain.ListItems has changed from 1 to 0. Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="A3B628A0-A810-4AE2-BFA2-9E7A29EB9AD0"'
		'UPGRADE_WARNING: MSComctlLib.IListItem method lvMain.ListItems.EnsureVisible has a new behavior. Click for more: 'ms-help://MS.VSCC.v80/dv_commoner/local/redirect.htm?keyword="6BA9B8D2-2A32-4B6E-8D36-44949974A5B4"'
		lvMain.Items.Item(lvMain.Items.Count).EnsureVisible()
		frm1st.LoadMainMenu()
		RaiseEvent GAMEOVER(Me, Nothing)
	End Sub
	
	
	Private Sub Select_Offense()
		frm1st.LoadOffenseMenu(team_name(p1))
		Wait(3, True)
	End Sub
	
	Private Sub Select_Defense()
		frm1st.LoadDefenseMenu(team_name(d))
		Wait(3, True)
	End Sub
	
	Private Sub Select_Running_Play()
		frm1st.LoadRunningPlays(team_name(p1))
		Wait(3, True)
	End Sub
	
	Private Sub Select_Pass_Coverage()
		frm1st.LoadPassCoverage(team_name(d))
		Wait(3, True)
	End Sub
	
	Private Sub Select_Ball_Carrier()
		frm1st.BuildBallCarriers(team_name(p1))
		Wait(3, True)
	End Sub
	
	Private Sub Select_Pass_Play()
		frm1st.LoadPassingPlays(team_name(p1))
		Wait(3, True)
	End Sub
	
	Private Sub Select_Gadget_Play()
		frm1st.LoadGadgetPlays(team_name(p1))
		Wait(3, True)
		
	End Sub
